I would be over the moon if you could help me and the kids for Christmas this year. Any donations of items you don't want or need out of your way. I know there's so many people out there struggling and I'm not the only one but I've been through so much in the past few years that I wish just one good thing could happen for us. I got my nieces out of a terrible situation and raising them. Things were good at first until I became sick and lost my job. I do cleaning jobs on the side and they help me on my really bad health days just to be able to keep a roof over our heads and things they absolutely need. More than anything I just wish I could get better and back to living my life and giving them the life they deserve. I have been trying to come up with something for Christmas for them and I either have a really bad health day and cant do extra cleaning jobs or something comes up like I had to replace a tire that keeps going flat, pay for school pictures and one had a school dance etc. I cant ever get ahead. I've called programs that help around Christmas time but they only help so many and all the spots are filled. It's the worst feeling to know I'll have nothing to give them Christmas morning and they don't understand because they're kids and it's not fair to them. I feel like such a failure because I was supposed to make things better for them and then I became sick out of nowhere and everything changed. My priority is keeping a roof over their heads, utilities on and food in their stomachs and I'm doing that just barely but I know they will be sad and so will I if I can't make something happen by Christmas. And I know this is so annoying but there's nothing I wouldn't do for them and I can at least try and hope that maybe you might see this and decide you would like to help a family in desperate need who would be more grateful and appreciative than you could ever know. I'm just asking if you have anything that you were going to donate, throw out, sell for a penny lol I can afford that! Etc please consider me and my girls. It can even be used items. I just want to make them happy. I would record the excitement and smiles on their faces and probably tears coming from mine if something happened.
